---

This is a self-contained version of some solutions for HoTT-Book's exercises.
The idea is to unpackage all as long as possible to get a better understanding.
Many changes can appear running this experiment. Solutions are
type-checked as a whole using Agda v2.5.3.

## Requirements

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Agda has a pragma to work with HoTT:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="563" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="567" class="Keyword">OPTIONS</a> <a id="575" class="Option">--without-K</a> <a id="587" class="Symbol">#-}</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Equality type definition also called Identity type:

## Chapter 1

### Exercise 1.1

{: .exercise}
  Given functions $$f : A \to B$$ and $$g:B\to C$$, define
  their composite $$ g\circ f:A\to C$$.
  Show that we have $$h \circ (g\circ f) \equiv (h\circ g)\circ f$$.


We define the composition operation in Agda as follows.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="_∘_"></a><a id="2160" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2160" class="Function Operator">_∘_</a> <a id="2164" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2166" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="2168" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2169" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2169" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="2171" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2171" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="2173" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2173" class="Bound">k</a><a id="2174" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="2176" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2177" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2177" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="2179" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2181" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="2185" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2169" class="Bound">i</a><a id="2186" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="2188" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2188" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="2190" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2192" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="2196" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2171" class="Bound">j</a><a id="2197" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="2199" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2199" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="2201" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2203" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="2207" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2173" class="Bound">k</a><a id="2208" class="Symbol">}</a>

### Exercise 1.2

<div class="exercise">
Derive the recursion principle for products $$\mathsf{rec}_{A\times B}$$
using only the projections, and verify that the definitional equalities
are valid. Do the same for $$\Sigma$$-types.
</div>

To solve this problem we need to know:

  - The recursion principle for Σ-types:

    <p class="equation">
    $$ \mathsf{rec}_{ A \times B}
      : \prod\limits_{C : \mathcal{U}} (A \to B \to C) → A \times B \to C.
    $$
    </p>

  - The recursion principle for Σ-types:

    <p class="equation">
    $$ \mathsf{rec}_{\sum\limits_{(x : A) } B(x)}
      : \prod\limits_{(C : U)} (\Pi_{(x : A)} B(x) \rightarrow C) \rightarrow
        \sum_{(x : A)} B(x) \rightarrow C
    $$
    </p>

<div class="proof" id="proof-1.2">
Proof.<br/>
For products:<br/>
If we have the projections,
$$\mathsf{proj}_1 : A \times B \to \mathsf{A}$$ and $$\mathsf{proj}_2 : A \times B \to \mathsf{B}$$,
then $$\mathsf{rec}_2$$ is another inhabitant where

<p class="equation">
$$
\begin{align*}
&\mathsf{rec}_1 : \prod\limits_{C : \mathcal{U}} (A \to B \to C) \to A \times B \to C\\
&\mathsf{rec}_1~C~g~c~:\equiv~g~(\mathsf{proj}_1 c,~\mathsf{proj}_2 c).
\end{align*}
$$
</p>
By reflexivity, we prove the equality between $$\mathsf{rec}_{ A \times B}$$ and $$\mathsf{rec}_1$$.
<br/>
<br/>
For sums:<br/>
The projections are $$\mathsf{proj}_1 : \sum_{x : A}  Bx \to \mathsf{A}$$ and
$$\mathsf{proj}_2 :  \prod_{(p : \sum_{x : A}  Bx)} \to \mathsf{B} (\mathsf{proj}_1 p)$$.<br/>
By using these projections, we got another recursor defined as follows:
<p class="equation">
$$
\begin{aling*}
&\mathsf{rec}_2 : \prod\limits_{C : \mathcal{U}}  (\prod_{x : A} Bx \to C) \to \sum\limits_{x : A} B x \to C\\
&\mathsf{rec}_2~C~g~c~=~g~(\mathsf{proj}_1 c)~(\mathsf{proj}_2 c)
\end{align*}
$$
</p>

By reflexivity, we prove the equality between $$\mathsf{rec}_{\sum\limits_{(x : A) } B(x)}$$ and $$\mathsf{rec}_2$$.
</div>

In Agda.<br>

Let's add some machinery to handle levels of the universe needed for
the following exercises including this one:

    <a id="5037" class="Keyword">constructor</a> <a id="Σ-Def₁.Σ._,_"></a><a id="5049" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#5049" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a>
    <a id="5057" class="Keyword">field</a>
      <a id="Σ-Def₁.Σ.proj₁"></a><a id="5069" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#5069" class="Field">proj₁</a> <a id="5075" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5077" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4986" class="Bound">A</a>

  <a id="5104" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="5109" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4977" class="Module">Σ</a> <a id="5111" class="Keyword">public</a>
<a id="5118" class="Comment">-- _,_ : (proj₁ : A) → B proj₁ → Σ A B.</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Its recursor with a function $$g : \prod_{(x : A)} B(x)\rightarrow C$$
that we provide.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

On the other hand, the product type is just a particular case of the sigma type
when the codomain is not dependent, as we can see next by omitting the argument
in `(λ _ → B)`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="5823" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="×-Def₁"></a><a id="5830" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#5830" class="Module">×-Def₁</a> <a id="5837" class="Keyword">where</a>

Its recursor with a function $$g : A \rightarrow B \rightarrow C$$ that we provide.

### Exercise 1.3

<p class="exercise">
Derive the induction principle for products $$\mathsf{ind}_{A\times B}$$,
using only the projections and the propositional uniqueness principle
$$\mathsf{uniq}_{A\times B}$$.
Verify that the definitional equalities are valid.
</p>

To solve this problem, recall the uniqueness principle (Pp. 29. HoTT-Book)

- The **propositional uniqueness principle** says that
every element of $$A\times B$$ is equal to a pair.

<p class="equation">
  $$ \mathsf{uniq}_{A\times B}
     : \prod_{(x : A \times B)} ((\mathsf{proj}_{1}(x) , \mathsf{proj}_{2}(x))
       \equiv_{A\times B} x).
  $$
</p>

Product type definition using `data`:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="6992" class="Comment">-- this would be trivial in agda due to definitional η for records</a>
<a id="7059" class="Comment">-- so Capriotti defined a product type without η:</a>

Projections and $$\mathsf{uniq}_{A\times B}$$:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="7448" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="×-Fun₂"></a><a id="7455" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7455" class="Module">×-Fun₂</a> <a id="7462" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7463" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7463" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="7465" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7465" class="Bound">j</a><a id="7466" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="7468" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7468" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="7470" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7472" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="7476" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7463" class="Bound">i</a><a id="7477" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="7479" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7479" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="7481" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7483" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="7487" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7465" class="Bound">j</a><a id="7488" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7490" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="7498" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="7503" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7116" class="Module">×-Def₂</a> <a id="7510" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="7516" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="7518" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7137" class="Datatype Operator">_×_</a><a id="7521" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="7522" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7193" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a><a id="7525" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="7527" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7216" class="Function">proj₁</a><a id="7532" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="7534" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7297" class="Function">proj₂</a><a id="7539" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="7544" class="Comment">-- propositional uniqueness principle:</a>

        <a id="7955" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7957" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7928" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7959" href="{%   <a id="7993" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7905" class="Function">pair=</a> <a id="7999" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#815" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="8004" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#815" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="8009" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8011" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#815" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The induction principle for the product type:

<p class="equation">
$$\mathsf{ind}_{A\times B} : \prod\limits_{C : A \times B \to \mathcal{U}}
  \left( \prod\limits_{x:A}\ \prod\limits_{y:B}\ \,C( (x,y) ) \right)
  \to \prod\limits_{x:A \times B}\ \,C(x)
$$
</p>

  <a id="8355" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="8360" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7116" class="Module">×-Def₂</a> <a id="8367" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="8373" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8374" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7137" class="Datatype Operator">_×_</a><a id="8377" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="8379" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7193" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a><a id="8382" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="8383" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7216" class="Function">proj₁</a><a id="8388" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="8389" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7297" class="Function">proj₂</a><a id="8394" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="×-Ind₂.ind"></a><a id="8426" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8426" class="Function">ind</a> <a id="8430" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8432" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="8434" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8435" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8435" class="Bound">k</a><a id="8436" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="8438" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8438" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="8440" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8442" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8325" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="8444" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7137" class="Datatype Operator">×</a> <a id="8446" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8336" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="8448" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8450" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="8454" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8435" class="Bound">k</a><a id="8455" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="8465" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8467" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="8469" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8469" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="8471" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8473" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8325" class="Bound">A</a><a id="8474" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="8476" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8476" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="8478" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8480" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8336" class="Bound">B</a><a id="8481" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8483" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8485" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8438" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="8487" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8488" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8469" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="8490" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7193" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="8492" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8476" class="Bound">y</a><a id="8493" class="Symbol">))</a>

<p class="exercise">
Generalize $$\mathsf{uniq}_{A\times B}$$ to Σ-types, and do the same for
$$\Sigma$$-types, i.e. show induction and verify the definitional equality
is valid.
</p>

Σ-type definition using `data`:

Projections and uniqueness propositional principle:

  <a id="9863" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9712" class="Function">ind-β</a> <a id="9869" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9869" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="9871" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9871" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="9873" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9873" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9875" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9875" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="9877" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9879" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#815" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

### Exercise 1.4

<div class="exercise">
Assuming as given only the <em>iterator</em> for natural numbers
<p class="equation">
$$\mathsf{ite} : \prod\limits_{C:\mathcal{U}} C \to (C \to C) \to \mathbb{N} \to C $$
</p>
with the defining equations
<p class="equation">
$$
\begin{align*}
\mathsf{ite}(C,c_0,c_s,0)               &\equiv c_0, \\
\mathsf{ite}(C,c_0,c_s,\mathsf{suc}(n)) &\equiv c_s(\mathsf{ite}(C,c_0,c_s,n)),
\end{align*}
$$
</p>
derive a function having the type of the recursor $$\mathsf{rec}$$.
Show that the defining equations of the recursor hold propositionally for this
function, using the induction principle for $$\mathbb{N}$$.
</div>

To solve this problem, let us define the recursor and also the induction principle
for natural numbers. (See more details about these functions in
[Induction on Natural Numbers]({% post_url 2018-02-12-induction-on-natural-numbers %})).

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="10803" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="ℕ-Def"></a><a id="10810" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10810" class="Module">ℕ-Def</a> <a id="10816" class="Keyword">where</a>

Now, we define the iterator following the equations above:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="11323" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="ℕ-Fun"></a><a id="11330" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11330" class="Module">ℕ-Fun</a> <a id="11336" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="11344" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="11349" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10810" class="Module">ℕ-Def</a> <a id="11355" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="11361" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11362" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10830" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="11363" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="11365" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10848" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a><a id="11369" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="11371" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10861" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a><a id="11374" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="11378" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="11383" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10882" class="Module">ℕ-Rec</a> <a id="11389" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="11395" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11396" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10909" class="Function">rec</a><a id="11399" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="ℕ-Fun.ite"></a><a id="11404" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11404" class="Function">ite</a> <a id="11408" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11410" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="11412" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11413" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11413" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="11415" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11417" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="11420" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11422" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11424" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11413" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="11426" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11428" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11429" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11413" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="11431" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11433" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11413" class="Bound">C</a><a id="11434" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11436" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11438" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10830" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="11440" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11442" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11413" class="Bound">C</a>
  <a id="11446" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11404" class="Function">ite</a> <a id="11450" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11450" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="11452" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11452" class="Bound">c₀</a> <a id="11455" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11455" class="Bound">cₛ</a> <a id="11458" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10848" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a>    <a id="11466" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11468" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11452" class="Bound">c₀</a>
  <a id="11473" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11404" class="Function">ite</a> <a id="11477" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11477" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="11479" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11479" class="Bound">c₀</a> <a id="11482" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11482" class="Bound">cₛ</a> <a id="11485" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11486" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10861" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="11490" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11490" class="Bound">n</a><a id="11491" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11493" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11495" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11482" class="Bound">cₛ</a> <a id="11498" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11499" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11404" class="Function">ite</a> <a id="11503" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11477" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="11505" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11479" class="Bound">c₀</a> <a id="11508" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11482" class="Bound">cₛ</a> <a id="11511" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11490" class="Bound">n</a><a id="11512" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Then, we now can define the recursor using this `ite` by iterating over the type
`ℕ × C` (*reloading recursion*?).


<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="11656" class="Comment">-- recursor</a>
  <a id="11670" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="11675" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7116" class="Module">×-Def₂</a> <a id="11682" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="11688" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11689" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7137" class="Datatype Operator">_×_</a><a id="11692" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="11694" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7216" class="Function">proj₁</a><a id="11699" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="11701" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7297" class="Function">proj₂</a><a id="11706" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="11708" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7193" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a><a id="11711" class="Symbol">)</a>

           <a id="11909" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11782" class="Bound">n</a><a id="11910" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Now, we need to establish the propositional equality between these two
definitions of recursor, i.e, between `rec` and `rec₂`. Let's use
induction to prove that.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="12100" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="ex1-4"></a><a id="12107" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12107" class="Module">ex1-4</a> <a id="12113" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="12122" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="12127" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10810" class="Module">ℕ-Def</a> <a id="12133" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="12139" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12140" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10830" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="12141" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="12143" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10848" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a><a id="12147" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="12149" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10861" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a><a id="12152" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="12156" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="12161" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10882" class="Module">ℕ-Rec</a> <a id="12167" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="12173" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12174" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10909" class="Function">rec</a><a id="12177" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="12181" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="12186" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11033" class="Module">ℕ-Ind</a> <a id="12192" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="12198" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12199" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11060" class="Function">ind</a><a id="12202" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="12206" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="12211" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11330" class="Module">ℕ-Fun</a> <a id="12217" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="12223" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12224" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11404" class="Function">ite</a><a id="12227" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="12229" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11716" class="Function">rec₂</a><a id="12233" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="12238" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="12243" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7116" class="Module">×-Def₂</a> <a id="12250" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="12256" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12257" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7137" class="Datatype Operator">_×_</a><a id="12260" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="12262" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7216" class="Function">proj₁</a><a id="12267" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="12269" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7297" class="Function">proj₂</a><a id="12274" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="12276" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7193" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a><a id="12279" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="ex1-4.proof"></a><a id="12298" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12298" class="Function">proof</a> <a id="12304" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12306" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12307" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12307" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="12309" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12311" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="12314" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="12316" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12316" class="Bound">c₀</a> <a id="12319" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12321" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12307" class="Bound">C</a><a id="12322" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="12324" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12324" class="Bound">cₛ</a> <a id="12327" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12329" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10830" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="12331" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12333" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12307" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="12335" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12337" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12307" class="Bound">C</a><a id="12338" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="12348" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12350" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="12352" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12353" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link ### Exercise 1.5

<div class="exercise">

Show that if we define

  $$A+B :\equiv \sum\limits_{(x : \mathbbbold{2})} \mathsf{rec}_{\mathbbbold{2}} (\mathcal{U}, A , B, x),$$

then we can give a definition of $$\ind\limits_{A + B}$$ for which the
definitional equalities holds.

</div>

To solve this problem, let us introduce the $$\mathcal{2}$$ type, that is, the
type with two constructors also called **Bool**. The constructors are also called
false and true respectively.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="13350" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="𝟚-Def₁"></a><a id="13357" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13357" class="Module">𝟚-Def₁</a> <a id="13364" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="13373" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="𝟚-Def₁.𝟚"></a><a id="13378" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13378" class="Datatype">𝟚</a> <a id="13380" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13382" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="13386" class="Keyword">where</a>
    <a id="𝟚-Def₁.𝟚.𝟘"></a><a id="13396" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13396" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟘</a> <a id="13398" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13400" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13378" class="Datatype">𝟚</a>
    <a id="𝟚-Def₁.𝟚.𝟙"></a><a id="13406" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13406" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟙</a> <a id="13408" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13410" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13378" class="Datatype">𝟚</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


With the recursor:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="13458" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="𝟚-Rec₁"></a><a id="13465" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13465" class="Module">𝟚-Rec₁</a> <a id="13472" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="13481" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="13486" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13357" class="Module">𝟚-Def₁</a>  <a id="13494" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="13500" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13501" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13396" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟘</a><a id="13502" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="13503" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13406" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟙</a><a id="13504" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="13505" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13378" class="Datatype">𝟚</a><a id="13506" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="14264" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14225" class="Function">inr</a> <a id="14268" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14268" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="14270" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14272" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14273" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13406" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟙</a> <a id="14275" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#5049" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="14277" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14268" class="Bound">b</a><a id="14278" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


Now, let's try to define the recursor for this coproduct, and later,
we'll try the dependent version of it to complete the exercise.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="14440" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="+-Rec₁"></a><a id="14447" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14447" class="Module">+-Rec₁</a> <a id="14454" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="14463" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="14468" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13912" class="Module">+-Def₁</a> <a id="14475" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="14481" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14482" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14032" class="Function Operator">_+_</a><a id="14485" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="14487" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14167" class="Function">inl</a><a id="14490" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="14491" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14225" class="Function">inr</a><a id="14494" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="14495" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#5049" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a><a id="14498" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="14502" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="14507" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13357" class="Module">𝟚-Def₁</a> <a id="14514" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="14520" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14521" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13396" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟘</a><a id="14522" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="14523" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13406" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟙</a><a id="14524" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="14525" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13378" class="Datatype">𝟚</a><a id="14526" class="Symbol">)</a>

      <a id="14577" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14579" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14580" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14546" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14582" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14584" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14560" class="Bound">C</a><a id="14585" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="14593" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14595" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14596" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14548" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="14598" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14600" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14560" class="Bound">C</a><a id="14601" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="14609" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14611" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14546" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14613" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14032" class="Function Operator">+</a> <a id="14615" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14548" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="14617" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14619" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14560" class="Bound">C</a>
  <a id="14623" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14531" class="Function">rec</a> <a id="14627" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14627" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14629" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14629" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14631" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14632" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13396" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟘</a> <a id="14634" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#5049" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="14636" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14636" class="Bound">a</a><a id="14637" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14639" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14641" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14627" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14643" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14636" class="Bound">a</a>
  <a id="14647" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14531" class="Function">rec</a> <a id="14651" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14651" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14653" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14653" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14655" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14656" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13406" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟙</a> <a id="14658" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#5049" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="14660" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14660" class="Bound">b</a><a id="14661" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14663" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14665" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14653" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14667" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14660" class="Bound">b</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Notice how the recursor of the coproduct matches with the elimination
rule of the disjunction conective also called *case analysis*. That's follows from the
[**propositions-as-types**](https://ncatlab.org/nlab/show/propositions+as+types).

![path](/assets/latexit-images/disj-elimination.png){: width="%50" }

Finally, the induction principle for the coproduct:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="15057" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="+-Ind₁"></a><a id="15064" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15064" class="Module">+-Ind₁</a> <a id="15071" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="15080" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="15085" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13912" class="Module">+-Def₁</a> <a id="15092" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="15098" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15099" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14032" class="Function Operator">_+_</a><a id="15102" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="15104" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14167" class="Function">inl</a><a id="15107" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="15108" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14225" class="Function">inr</a><a id="15111" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="15113" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#5049" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a><a id="15116" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="15120" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="15125" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13357" class="Module">𝟚-Def₁</a> <a id="15132" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="15138" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15139" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13396" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟘</a><a id="15140" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="15141" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13406" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟙</a><a id="15142" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="15143" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13378" class="Datatype">𝟚</a><a id="15144" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="+-Ind₁.ind"></a><a id="15149" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15149" class="Function">ind</a> <a id="15153" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15155" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="15157" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15158" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15158" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="15160" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15160" class="Bound">j</a><a id="15161" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15163" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15164" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15164" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="15166" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15166" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="15168" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15170" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="15174" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15158" class="Bound">i</a><a id="15175" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15177" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15178" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15178" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="15180" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15182" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15164" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="15184" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14032" class="Function Operator">+</a> <a id="15186" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15166" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="15188" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15190" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="15194" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15160" class="Bound">j</a><a id="15195" class="Symbol">}</a>
      <a id="15203" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15205" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="15207" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15207" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="15209" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15211" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15164" class="Bound">A</a><a id="15212" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15214" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15216" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15178" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="15218" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15219" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14167" class="Function">inl</a> <a id="15223" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15207" class="Bound">a</a><a id="15224" class="Symbol">))</a>
      <a id="15233" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15235" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="15237" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15237" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="15239" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15241" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15166" class="Bound">B</a><a id="15242" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15244" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15246" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15178" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="15248" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15249" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14225" class="Function">inr</a> <a id="15253" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15237" class="Bound">b</a><a id="15254" class="Symbol">))</a>

### Exercise 1.6

<div class="exercise" id="ex-1.6">
Show that if we define $$A \times B :≡ \prod_{x:\mathbf{2}}\mathsf{rec}_{\mathbf{2}}\ (\mathcal{U}\, A\, B\, x)$$,
then we can give a definition of $$\mathsf{ind}_{A\times B}$$ for which the definitional
equalities propositionally (i.e. using equality types).
</div>

  <a id="16083" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="16088" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13357" class="Module">𝟚-Def₁</a> <a id="16095" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="16101" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16102" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13396" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟘</a><a id="16103" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="16104" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13406" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟙</a><a id="16105" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="16106" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13378" class="Datatype">𝟚</a><a id="16107" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16109" class="Keyword">public</a>

### Exercise 1.8

<div class="exercise" id="exercise-1.8">

Define multiplication and exponentiation using $$\mathsf{rec}{\mathbb{N}}$$.
Verify that $$(\mathbb{N},+,0,\times,1)$$ is a semiring using only
$$\ind{\mathbb{N}}$$.

</div>


<div class="proof" markdown="1">
Solution.<br/>
Operation definitions:

}}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#18192" class="Bound">m</a> <a id="18194" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18196" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10830" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="18197" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18199" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18201" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10830" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="18202" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18204" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="18207" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#18207" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="18209" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18211" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10861" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="18215" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10848" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a><a id="18219" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18221" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="18224" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#18224" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="18226" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#18226" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="18228" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#18228" class="Bound">m</a> <a id="18230" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18232" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#18067" class="Function">multi</a> <a id="18238" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#18228" class="Bound">m</a> <a id="18240" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18241" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#18226" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="18243" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#18228" class="Bound">m</a><a id="18244" class="Symbol">))</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

On the other hand, a **semiring** is a type? together with two binary operators S(+,*) satisfying the following conditions:

1. Additive associativity: $$\prod_{a,b,c : S} (a+b)+c=a+(b+c)$$.

2. Additive commutativity: $$\prod_{a,b : S}  a+b=b+a$$.

3. Multiplicative associativity: $$\prod_{a,b,c : S} (a*b)*c=a*(b*c)$$.

4. Left and right distributivity:

$$\prod_{a,b,c : S} a*(b+c)=(a*b)+(a*c)\text{  and  } \prod_{a,b,c : S} (b+c)*a=(b*a)+(c*a).$$

</div>

### Exercise 1.9

<div class="exercise" id="exercise-1.9">

Define the type family $$\mathsf{Fin} : \mathbb{N} \to \mathcal{U}$$ mentioned
at the end of Section 1.3, and the dependent function $$\mathsf{fmax} :
\prod_{n:\mathbb{N}} \mathsf{Fin}(n+1)$$ mentioned in Section 1.4.
</div>

### Exercise 1.11

<div class="exercise" id="exercise-1.11">
Show that for any type $$A$$, we have $$\neg\neg\neg A \to \neg A$$.
</div>

A propositional logic proof using [Agda-Prop](http://github.com/jonaprieto/agda-prop)
library:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="20173" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Ex1-11"></a><a id="20180" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20180" class="Module">Ex1-11</a> <a id="20187" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="20195" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="20200" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="20207" href="Data.PropFormula.html" class="Module">Data.PropFormula</a> <a id="20224" class="Number">1</a>

  <a id="Ex1-11.proof"></a><a id="20229" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20229" class="Function">proof</a> <a id="20235" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20237" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="20239" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20240" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20240" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="20241" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20243" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20244" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20244" class="Bound">A</a><a id="20245" class="Symbol">}</a>
        <a id="20255" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20257" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20240" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="20259" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1657" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="20261" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20263" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20265" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20267" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20244" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="20269" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#919" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⊃</a> <a id="20271" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20273" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20244" class="Bound">A</a>
  <a id="20277" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20229" class="Function">proof</a> <a id="20283" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20284" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20284" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="20285" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="20287" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20287" class="Bound">A</a><a id="20288" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20290" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="20296" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#3276" class="InductiveConstructor">⊃-intro</a>
      <a id="20310" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20311" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#2276" class="InductiveConstructor">¬-intro</a>
          <a id="20329" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20330" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#2387" class="InductiveConstructor">¬-elim</a>
              <a id="20351" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20352" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1868" class="InductiveConstructor">weaken</a> <a id="20359" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20287" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="20361" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20362" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1706" class="InductiveConstructor">assume</a> <a id="20369" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20370" class="Argument">Γ</a> <a id="20372" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="20374" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20284" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="20375" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20377" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20378" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20380" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20381" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20383" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20384" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20386" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20287" class="Bound">A</a><a id="20387" class="Symbol">)))))</a>
              <a id="20407" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20408" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#2276" class="InductiveConstructor">¬-intro</a>
                <a id="20432" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20433" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#2387" class="InductiveConstructor">¬-elim</a>
                  <a id="20458" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20459" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1706" class="InductiveConstructor">assume</a> <a id="20466" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20467" class="Argument">Γ</a> <a id="20469" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="20471" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20284" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="20473" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1170" class="Function Operator">,</a> <a id="20475" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20477" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20479" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20481" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20287" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="20483" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1170" class="Function Operator">,</a> <a id="20485" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20287" class="Bound">A</a><a id="20486" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20488" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20489" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20491" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20287" class="Bound">A</a><a id="20492" class="Symbol">))</a>
                  <a id="20513" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20514" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1868" class="InductiveConstructor">weaken</a> <a id="20521" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20522" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20524" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20287" class="Bound">A</a><a id="20525" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20527" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20528" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1706" class="InductiveConstructor">assume</a> <a id="20535" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20536" class="Argument">Γ</a> <a id="20538" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="20540" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20284" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="20542" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1170" class="Function Operator">,</a> <a id="20544" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20546" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20548" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20550" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20287" class="Bound">A</a><a id="20551" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20553" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20287" class="Bound">A</a><a id="20554" class="Symbol">))))))</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

In type theory, the term is:

$$
λ (x : ((A → ⊥) → ⊥) → ⊥) (a : A) . x ((λ h : A → ⊥) . ha) :
((A → ⊥) → ⊥) → ⊥) → (A → ⊥)
$$

### Exercise 1.16

<div class="exercise" id="exercise-1.16">
Show that addition of natural numbers is commutative:
<p class="equation">
$$
\prod\limits_{i,j : \mathbb{N}}\ (i + j = j + i).
$$
</p>
</div>

Hint: by induction twice.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="20945" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Ex1-16"></a><a id="20952" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20952" class="Module">Ex1-16</a> <a id="20959" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="20967" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="20972" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10810" class="Module">ℕ-Def</a>
  <a id="20980" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="20985" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11033" class="Module">ℕ-Ind</a>
  <a id="20993" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="20998" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#17961" class="Module">Ex1-8</a> <a id="21004" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="21010" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21011" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#18002" class="Function Operator">_+_</a><a id="21014" class="Symbol">)</a>

                      <a id="21762" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#21577" class="Bound">hyp₂</a><a id="21766" class="Symbol">)))</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Chapter 2

### Exercise 2.6

<div class="exercise" id="exercise-2.6">
Prove that if $$p : x \equiv y$$, then the function
$$(p \cdot -) : (y \equiv z) \to (x \equiv z)$$ is an equivalence.
</div>

![path-triangle](/assets/ipe-images/path-triangle.png){: width="%50" }

<div class="proof">
Solution. <br/>

To show the equivalence, it sufficies to show a function
$$g : x \equiv z \to y \equiv z$$ such that we can prove
$$ (p \cdot -) \circ g \sim \mathsf{id}_{x \equiv z}$$ and
$$ g \circ (p \cdot -) \sim \mathsf{id}_{y \equiv z}$$.

Let's define the function $$g$$.
<p class="equation">
$$
\begin{align*}
&g : x ≡ z → y ≡ z\\
&g~m~=~\mathsf{trans}~(\mathsf{sym}~p)~m
\end{align*}
$$
</p>
<br/>

($$(p \cdot -) \circ g \sim \mathsf{id}_{x \equiv z}$$):
Let be $$m : x ≡ z$$, we have,

<p class="equation">
$$
\begin{align*}
(p \cdot -) \circ g (m) &= (p \cdot -)~(g~m)\\
                        &= (p \cdot -)~(\mathsf{trans}~(\mathsf{sym}~p)~m)\\
                        &= \mathsf{trans}~p~(\mathsf{trans}~(\mathsf{sym}~p)~m)\\
                        &= \mathsf{trans}~(\mathsf{trans}~p~(\mathsf{sym}~p))~m\\
                        &= \mathsf{trans}~\mathsf{refl}_{x≡z}~m\\
                        &= m
\end{align*}
$$
</p>
<br/>
($$ g \circ (p \cdot -) \sim \mathsf{id}_{y \equiv z}$$):
Let be $$n : y ≡ z$$, we have,

<p class="equation">
$$
\begin{align*}
g \circ (p \cdot -) n &= g (\mathsf{trans}~p~n)\\
                      &= (\mathsf{trans}~(\mathsf{sym}~p)~(\mathsf{trans}~p~n)\\
                      &= \mathsf{trans}~(\mathsf{trans}~(\mathsf{sym}~p)~p)~n\\
                      &= \mathsf{trans}~\mathsf{refl}_{y ≡ z}~n\\
                      &= n.
\end{align*}
$$
</p>

</div>


### Exercise 2.10

<div class="exercise" id="exercise-2.10">
Prove that ∑-types are associative, in that for any $$A : \mathcal{U}$$
and families $$B : A  \to U$$ and $$C : \sum_{(x : A)} B(x) \to \mathcal{U}$$,
we have
<p class="equation">
$$\sum\limits_{(x : A)} \sum\limits_{(y : B(x))} C((x,y)) \simeq \sum\limits_{p : \sum_{x:A} B(x)} C(p)$$.
</p>
</div>

<div class="proof" id="proof-2.10">
Solution.<br/>
We can prove that the following functions $$f$$ and $$g$$ are inverses.

<p class="equation">
$$\sum\limits_{(x : A)} \sum\limits_{(y : B(x))} C((x,y)) \overset{f}{\underset{g}{\rightleftarrows}} \sum\limits_{p : \sum_{x:A} B(x)} C(p)$$.
</p>
defined by $$f(a,b,c) :\equiv ((a,b),c)$$ and $$g(z,c) :\equiv (\mathsf{proj}_1 z,\mathsf{proj}_{2} z, c)$$.<br/>
Indeed,
<p class="equation">
$$
\begin{align*}
(f \circ g) (z, c) &:\equiv f (g (z,c))\\
&:\equiv f\,(\mathsf{proj}_1 z,\mathsf{proj}_{2} z, c)\\
&:\equiv ((\mathsf{proj}_1 z,\mathsf{proj}_{2} z), c)
\end{align*}
$$
</p>
</div>

  <a id="Σ-Fun₁.f-g"></a><a id="24863" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#24863" class="Function">f-g</a> <a id="24867" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24869" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="24871" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24872" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#24872" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24874" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24876" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="24879" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24881" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24882" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#24882" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24884" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24886" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#24872" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24888" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24890" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="24893" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24895" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24896" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#24896" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="24898" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24900" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4977" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="24902" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#24872" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24904" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#24882" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24906" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24908" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="24911" class="Symbol">}</a>
        <a id="24921" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24923" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24924" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#24924" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="24926" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24928" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4977" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="24930" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24931" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4977" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="24933" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#24872" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24935" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#24882" class="Bound">B</a><a id="24936" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24938" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#24896" class="Bound">C</a><a id="24939" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="24949" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24951" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#24562" class="Function">f</a> <a id="24953" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24954" class="Argument">A</a> <a id="24956" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="24958" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#24872" class="Bound">A</a><a id="24959" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="24961" class="Argument">B</a> <a id="24963" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="24965" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#24882" class="Bound">B</a><a id="24966" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="24968" class="Argument">C</a> <a id="24970" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="24972" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#24896" class="Bound">C</a><a id="24973" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24975" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24976" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#24703" class="Function">g</a> <a id="24978" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#24924" class="Bound">x</a><a id="24979" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24981" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#767" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="24983" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#24924" class="Bound">x</a>
  <a id="24987" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#24863" class="Function">f-g</a> <a id="24991" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#24991" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="24993" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="24995" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#815" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>

  <a id="Σ-Fun₁.g-f"></a><a id="25003" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#25003" class="Function">g-f</a> <a id="25007" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="25009" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="25011" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="25012" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#25012" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="25014" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="25016" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="25019" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="25021" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="25022" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#25022" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="25024" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="25026" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#25012" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="25028" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="25030" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="25033" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="25035" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="25036" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#25036" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="25038" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="25040" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4977" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="25042" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#25012" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="25044" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#25022" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="25046" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="25048" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="25051" class="Symbol">}</a>
        <a id="25061" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="25063" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="25064" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#25064" ### Exercise 2.13

<div class="exercise" id="exercise-2.13">
Show that $$(2 \simeq 2) \simeq 2$$.
</div>

<div class="proof" markdown="1">
Solution.<br/>

The following text is from [jdoughertyii](https://github.com/jdoughertyii/hott-exercises/blob/master/Ch02.v).<br/>
The result essentially says that $$2$$ is equivalent to itself in two ways:
the identity provides one equivalence, and negation gives the other.  So we
first define these.  $$\mathsf{id}_{2}$$ is its own quasi-inverse; we have
$$\mathsf{id}_{2} \circ \mathsf{id}_{2} \equiv \mathsf{id}_{2}$$, so $$\mathsf{id}_{2}
\circ \mathsf{id}_{2}
\sim \mathsf{id}_{2}$$ easily.  $$\lnot$$ is also its own quasi-inverse, since for
any $$x$$, $$\lnot\lnot x = x$$.
To show the result, we need to map $$\mathsf{id}_{2}$$ and $$\lnot$$ onto $$2$$ is
a quasi-invertible way.  But we need to define this map on all of $$2
\simeq 2$$.  So for any $$h : 2\simeq 2$$, let $$f(h) = h(0_{2})$$,
and define $$g : 2 \to (2 \simeq 2)$$ by

$$
  g(0_{2}) = \mathsf{id}_{2}
  \qquad\qquad
  g(1_{2}) = \lnot
$$

To show that these are quasi-inverses,
note first that whatever else is the case, an equivalence
$$2 \simeq 2$$ can't be a constant function, which we can prove by a case
analysis.  Each of $$f(0_{2})$$ and $$f(1_{2})$$ is in $$2$$, so it is
either $$0_{2}$$ or $$1_{2}$$.  So we have the cases:
 - $$f(0_{2}) = f(1_{2})$$, in which case we can apply $$f^{-1}$$ to either side to get a contradiction, or
 - $$f(0_{2}) = \lnot f(1_{2})$$. In which case we have the result
Showing that $$f \circ g \sim \mathsf{id}_{2}$$ is easy, since we can do it by
cases.  We have

$$\begin{align*}
  f(g(0_{2})) &= f(\mathsf{id}_{2}) = \mathsf{id}_{2}(0_{2}) = 0_{2}
  \\
  f(g(1_{2})) &= f(\lnot) = \lnot 0_{2} = 1_{2}
\end{align*}%
$$

For the other direction, suppose that $$h : 2 \simeq 2$$ and that
function extensionality holds.
$$h(0_{2})$$ is either $$0_{2}$$ or $$1_{2}$$.  If the first, then
because $$h$$ isn't constant we have $$h(1_{2}) = \lnot h(0_{2}) =
1_{2}$$, hence $$h = \mathsf{id}_{2}$$.  Furthermore,
$$
  g(f(h)) = g(h(0_{2})) = g(0_{2}) = \mathsf{id}_{2} = h
$$
The same argument works for the other case.  So $$f$$ is an equivalence, and
$$(2 \simeq 2) \simeq 2$$.

</div>

### Exercise 2.14

<div class="exercise">

  Suppose we add to type theory <a
  href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=IlfQjWqrK6I">the equality reflection
  rule</a> which says that if there is an element $$p : \mathsf{Id}(x,y) $$,
  then in fact $$ x :\equiv y$$. Prove that for any $$p : \mathsf{Id}(x,x)$$ we
  have $$p \equiv \mathsf{refl}_x$$.

  <p class="equation">
  $$
    \begin{prooftree}
    \AxiomC{$\vdash p : \mathsf{Id}(x, y)$}
    \RightLabel{$\mathsf{Eq}$}
    \UnaryInfC{$\vdash x \equiv y.$}
    \end{prooftree}
  $$
  </p>

</div>

<div class="proof">
  Proof.<br/>
  We first fix the type of $$\mathsf{refl}_x$$ in order to apply effectively
  path induction.<br/>

  <p class="equation">
    $$
    \begin{prooftree}
    \AxiomC{$x : A, y : A, p : x = y ⊢ p : x = y$}
    \RightLabel{$\mathsf{Eq}$}
    \UnaryInfC{$x : A, y : A, p : x = y ⊢ x ≡ y$}
    \AxiomC{$x : A, y : A, p : x = y ⊢ \mathsf{refl}_x : x = x$}
    \BinaryInfC{$x : A, y : A, p : x = y ⊢ \mathsf{refl}_x : x = y.$}
    \end{prooftree}
    $$
  </p>

  Now, $$\mathsf{refl}_x$$ and $$p : x = y$$ in the formulation of path induction
  are well-typed. Therefore, by path induction, we show that
  $$\mathsf{Id}(p,\mathsf{refl_{x}})$$. Let be $$x : A$$ and $$C :\equiv
  \prod_{y : A} \prod_{p : x \equiv y }\ p \equiv \mathsf{refl}_{x}$$.
  It sufficies to show and inhabitant of $$C(x, \mathsf{refl}_{x})$$, and this is
  $$\mathsf{refl}_{\mathsf{refl}_x} : \mathsf{refl}_x = \mathsf{refl}_x$$.
  By the equation reflection rule, since we have an inhabitant of $$p \equiv
  \mathsf{refl}_x$$, we conclude these terms are judgemental equal,i.e., $$p \equiv \mathsf{refl}_x$$.
</div>

### Exercise 2.17

<div class="exercise">
<ul>
  <li> Show that if $$A \simeq A$$  and $$B \simeq B'$$, then $$(A\times B) \simeq (A'\times B')$$. </li>
  <li> Give two proofs of this fact, one using univalence and one not using it, and show that the two proofs are equal.</li>
  <li> Formulate and prove analogous results for the other type formers: $$\Sigma$$, $$\to$$, $$\Pi$$, and $$+$$. </li>
</ul>
</div>

<div class="proof" markdown="1">
- Assuming univalence.
<br/>
$$
\begin{prooftree}
\AxiomC{$f : A \simeq A$}
\RightLabel{$\mathsf{ua}$}
\UnaryInfC{$A =_{\mathcal{U}} A$}
\AxiomC{$g : B \simeq B'$}
\RightLabel{$\mathsf{ua}$}
\UnaryInfC{$B =_{\mathcal{U}} B'$}
\RightLabel{$\mathsf{pair=}$}
\BinaryInfC{$(A\times B) =_{\mathcal{U}} (A'\times B')$}
\RightLabel{$\mathsf{idtoequiv}$}
\UnaryInfC{$(A\times B) \simeq (A'\times B')$}
\end{prooftree}
$$

- Without using univalence, it is easy to prove
that the function $$h$$ defined as follows gives us the
equivalence that we are looking for.

$$
\begin{align*}
&h : (A\times B) \to (A'\times B')\\
&h (a , b) = (f\, a, g\, b).
\end{align*}
$$

With the inverse:

$$
\begin{align*}
&h^{-1} : (A'\times B') \to (A\times B)\\
&h^{-1} (a , b) = (f^{-1}\, a, g^{-1}\, b).
\end{align*}
$$

To prove these proofs are equal it is sufficies to
show these underlyding functions are equal.


</div>

## Chapter 3

To solve the following exercises, let us recall a few things:

- The *set* definition in HoTT:

A type $$A$$ is a **set** if for all $$x, y : A$$ and
all $$p, q : x \equiv y$$, we have $$ p \equiv q$$. In a proposition
we have

$$
\mathsf{isSet}(A) :\equiv \prod\limits_{(x,y : A)}\prod\limits_{(p,q : x \equiv y)} (p \equiv q).
$$

- The type for equivalence from $$A$$ to $$B$$

$$
  (A \simeq B) :\equiv \sum\limits_{f : A \to B} \mathsf{isequiv}(f),
$$

where

$$
\mathsf{isequiv(f)} :\equiv
  \left (\sum\limits_{g : B \to A} (f \circ g \sim \mathsf{id}_{B})\right) \times
  \left (\sum\limits_{h : B \to A} (h \circ f \sim \mathsf{id}_{A})\right)
$$

- The homotopy concept:

Let $$f , g : \prod\limits_{(x:A)} P(x)$$ be two sections of a
type family $$P : A \to \mathcal{U}$$. A **homotopy** from $$f$$ to $$g$$
is a dependent function of type

$$
(f \sim g) :\equiv \prod\limits_{x : A} (f(x) \equiv g(x)).
$$

### Exercise 3.1

<div class="exercise">
Prove that if $$A\simeq B$$ and $$A$$ is a set, then so is $$B$$.
</div>


<div class="proof" id="proof-3.1" markdown="1" >
Proof 1.<br/>
Let be $$x,y : B$$ and $$p : x \equiv_{B} y$$ and $$q : x \equiv_{B} y$$.
We need to prove $$ p \equiv q$$.<br/>
Since $$A\simeq B$$ then there is a function $$f : A \to B$$ and some
$$g : B \to A$$ such that $$f \circ g \sim id_{B}$$.
Using this function $$g$$ over the path $$p$$ we get
$$\mathsf{ap}_{g} p : g x \equiv_{A} g y$$.
We do the same but this time over the path $$q$$, that is,
$$\mathsf{ap}_{g} q : g x \equiv_{A} g y$$.
Because of $$A$$ is a set, we have a new path called
$$m :\mathsf{ap}_{g} p \equiv_{gx \equiv_{A} gy} \mathsf{ap}_{g} q$$. <br/>

Now, an action over this path $$m$$
using the function $$\mathsf{ap}_{f} : x \equiv_{A} y \to f x \equiv_{B} f y$$
will give us


$$
\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{ap}_{f}} m :
(\mathsf{ap}_{f}) (\mathsf{ap}_{g} p) \equiv (\mathsf{ap}_{f})  (\mathsf{ap}_{g} q).
$$


By the lemmas in Chapter 2, we do the following reasoning:

$$
\begin{align*}
(\mathsf{ap}_{f}) (\mathsf{ap}_{g} p) \equiv (\mathsf{ap}_{f})  (\mathsf{ap}_{g} q) &=
  \mathsf{ap}_{f \circ g} p \equiv \mathsf{ap}_{f \circ g} q\\
  &=(\text{transporting by using} f \sim g)\\
  &=\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{id}_{B}} p \equiv \mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{id}_{B}} q\\
  &=p \equiv q.
\end{align*}
$$

Then, we have the inhabitant, $$\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{ap}_{f}} m : p \equiv q$$.
</div>

### Exercise 3.2

<div class="exercise">
Prove that if $$A$$ and $$B$$ are sets, then so is $$A+B$$.
</div>

To solve this exercise, we should take a look of some results from Chapter 2,
Section 2.12.

<div class="proof" id="proof-3.2" markdown="1">
Proof.<br/>

Let be $$x, y : A + B$$, and paths $$p : x \equiv y$$, $$q : x \equiv
y$$. Let's get a path $$p \equiv q$$.  We proceed by case analysis. If
$$x :\equiv \mathsf{inl} a$$ and $$y :\equiv \mathsf{inl} b$$, for
some $$a, b : A$$ then $$\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}^{-1}} p : a
\equiv_{A} b$$ and $$\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}^{-1}} q : a \equiv_{A}
b$$.

Since $$A$$ is a set, there is a path between these last two terms,
this is, $$m : \mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}^{-1}} p \equiv
\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}^{-1}} q$$.  Now, an action over this path
$$m$$ using the $$\mathsf{inl}$$ function give us:
$$\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}} m : \mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}}
(\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}^{-1}} p) \equiv \mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}}
(\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}^{-1}} q)$$.<br/>

By path algebra we have $$\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}}
m : p \equiv q$$ since $$\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}}
(\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}^{-1}} p) \equiv p$$.<br/> Following the
same reasoning, we prove the case $$x :\equiv \mathsf{inr} a$$ and $$y
:\equiv \mathsf{inr} b$$.  For the latest cases, $$x :\equiv
\mathsf{inl} a$$ and $$y :\equiv \mathsf{inr} b$$ and $$x :\equiv
\mathsf{inr} a$$ and $$y :\equiv \mathsf{inl} b$$, we use the
encode-decode method to derive a proof term for 𝟘 from
$$p$$ and $$q$$. Then, we may conclude anything we wish, that is, $$p
\equiv q$$.
</div>


### Exercise 3.4

<div class="exercise">
Show that $$A$$ is a mere proposition if and only
if $$A\to A$$ is contractible.
</div>

<div class="proof" markdown="1">
Proof. <br/>
- We must to show an inhabitant of the following type:

$$
\mathsf{isProp}(A) \to \sum\limits_{f : A \to A}\, \prod\limits_{g : A \to A } f = g.
$$

This is my proposed term:

$$
t :\equiv λ \mathsf{Aprop} \to (\mathsf{id}_{A}, λ (g : A \to A) \to \mathsf{funext} (\lambda (x : A) \to \mathsf{Aprop}~(\mathsf{id}~x)~(g~x)).
$$

- If $$A → A$$ is contractible, all functions in this type are equal,
then in particular given $$x, y : A$$, the constant functions $$f(w) \equiv x$$
and $$g(w) \equiv y$$ are equal. Then, $$\mathsf{happly} (f =_{A \to A} g, w) : x = y$$.
Therefore $$A$$ is a mere proposition.

</div>
